Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Bka'-gdams-pa: Contents
II. BKA' GDAMS
(Gnyis pa jo bo rje Dpal ldan A ti sha'i bka' srol las
byon pa'i BKA' GDAMS RIN PO CHE la gsum/ gzhung/ gdams pa/
man ngag go)
A. Dang po GZHUNG la
1. Rtsa ba Byang chub lam gyi sgron na Jo bo rjes mdzad
pa
2. De'i 'grel pa Byang chub lam gyi snang ba rab tu gsal
3. Sgam po lugs kyi lan rim Rtogs Idan Mkha' spyod dbang
pos mdzad pa
4. Skyes bu gsum gyi lam rim gyi khrid yig bdud rtsi'i
nying khu Rje btsun Tā ra nã thas mdzad pa
5. Lam rim bsdus don gyi tshigs bcad Rje rin po che Blo
bzang grags pa'i apal gyis mázad pa
Byang chub lam rim la thog mar blo sbyong ba chos kyi
sgo 'byed Rgya ma ba Blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa
Lam rim khrid gser zhun ma Rgyal ba Bsod nams rgya mtshos
mdzad pa
Lam rim dmar khrid zung 'jug bde lam Pan chen Blo bzang
chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa
9. Lam rim nyams su len pa'i tshul Rje bla ma rin po ches
mdzad pa
10. De'i cha lag theg pa chen po dbu ma lugs kyi sems
bskyed kyi cho ga byang chub gzhung lam
11. Theg pa chen po shin tu rgyas pa'i lugs kyi sems
bskyed cho ga byang chub lam bzang Rje bla ma 'Jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa
B. Gnyis pa GDAMS NGAG GI SKOR la.
1. Bya 'chad dka' ba Ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i Blo sbyong
don baun ma'i rtsa ba mchan bu dang bcas pa
2. Sems dpa' chen po Gzhon nu rgyal mchog gi mtshan gzhan
gzhan Dkon mchog 'bangs su grags pa dang Mus chen Dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan doon slobkyis Theg pa chen po'i
blo sbyong gi rgya gzhun bod gzhung shin tu gces pa
rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa Blo sbyong brgya rtsar
grags pa dkar chag rang gzhung du gsal ba itar tshang
ba
3. Blo sbyong (f. 33v) khrid yig Rgyal sras thogs med
bzang pos mdzad pa
4. Blo sbyong don bdun ma'i nyams len snying por dril ba
phan bde'i sa bon 'Jam dbyangs bla mas mdzad pa
5. Blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid yig nyams su len bder
bkod pa blodman 'jug bde
6. De'i brgyud 'debs
7. Smon lam gtan bde'i sa bon bcas
Gsum pa MAN NGAG GI SKOR la
1. Gsang chos glegs bam rin po che'i rtsa ba Byang sems
nor bu'i phreng ba
2. Thig le bou drug gi dbang chog
3. Bsgom bzlas nyams len snying por dril ba Dkon mchog
bstan pa'i sgron mes md zad pa
4. Khrid yig grub gnyis mchog sbyin Rje bla ma rin po ches
mdzad pa
5. Zhar byung bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang gi yi ge
Jo nang rin 'byung las khol phyungs bklag chog tu bkod
܀ ܟ݁ܢܽܘ ܕ݁ܪܽܬ݁ܘܺ ܟ݁ ܀ ܗ݁
6. Lha bzhi'i khrid yig mdo sngags lam gyi beud 'dus
7. Bka' gdams gsar ma'i mtshan gzhi lam gyi gtso bo rnam

gsum gyi rtsa ba Rje rin po che Blo bzang grags pas
mdzad pa
8. De'i rnam bshad go sla nyung 'dus skal bzang thar
pa'i 'jug ngogs
9. De dag gi rje 'brel du dge ldan phyag chen rgyal ba'i
gzhung lam Pan chen Blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan
gyis mdzad pa gzhung gsal byed bcas
10. Dbu ma'ilta khrid baud rtsi'i snying po Mang thos
Klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa
11. Gzhan stong dbu ma'i ita khrid rdo rje zla ba dri
ma med pa'i 'od
12. Byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga
thar pa'i lam sgron
13. Bka' srung mgon po gri gug ma'i rjes gnang gi yi ge
gsar bkod mams so

III. SA SKYA PA
(Gsum pa gsang sngags bstan pa'i mnga' bdag dpal ldan
sa skya pa'i gdams ngag gi gtso bo lam 'bras lam skor dang
bcas pa la gsum)
A. Dang po LAM BRAS BU DANG BCAS PA'I GZHUNG
1. Rtsa ba Rdo rje'i tshig rkang
2. De'i bsdus don mchan dang bcas pa
3. 'Khor 'das dbyer med kyi gzhung rtsa ba Rje btsun
Grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa
Gzhung ji lta ba (f. 34r) bzhin dkri ba'i khrid yig
jo lcags ma
5. Řnam 'grel don bsdus tshigs bcad ma mchan bcas
6. Yang tshigs bcad ma
7. De'i bsdus don mchan ma Ngor chen Kun dga' bzang pos
mdzad pa
8. Gzhung rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi 'grel pa gnyags ma
mchan can bcas
B. Gnyis pa SMIN BYED DBANG la
1. Kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi rgyu dbang la Ngor chen
Dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs
2. Dkyil chog
3. Gtor chog
4. Dbang bskur gyi phyag len bklags chog ma Ngor pa doon
slob 'Jam dbyangs Blo gter dbang pos mdzad pa bcas
c. Gsum pa GROL BYED KHRID la
1. Lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs
2. Ring brgyud lam ji lta ba bzhin tu dkri ba'i khrid
yig sbas don gsal ba dpal ldan bla ma dam pa Bsod
nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa
3. Nye brgyud lam sbas bshad dang/
4. Shin tu nye brgyud brda don gsal ba'i khrid yig Bdag
chen rdo rje 'chang Blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad
pa
5. (Phyi ma 'di kye rdor lugs kyi sbyor drug tu'ang
grags)
Lam 'bras phag gru lugs kyi khrid Stag lung thang pa
rin po ches zin bris mdzad pa
6. Bshad rgyud rdo rje gur gyi dgongs pa dag pa gsum gyi
khrid Chos rgyal Phags pas mdzad pa
'Grel pa lugs rtsa ba med pa'i lam 'bras su grags pa/
Lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi brgyud 'debs Ngor chen
gsung kha skong bcas
8. Dombhi he ru kas mdzad pa'i Lhan cig skyes grub mchan
dang bcas pa
9. Slob doon Padma badzra gyis mdzad pa'i Dpal kye rdo
rje'i mar me'i rtse mo ita bu'i gdams ngag rgya gzhung
10. Bskyed rim zab mo'i tshul dgu dang Rd zogs rim mar
me'i rtse mo lta bu'i gdams ngag Rje btsun Grags
pas mdzad pa
11. Nag po spyod pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i Gtum mo lam
rdzogs kyi gdams ngag Rje btsun Grags pas mdzad pa
12. Slob doon U tsi ta 'Chi ba med pas mdzad pa Rtsa
rlung thig le yon po srang ba'i man ngag gi lo rgyus
gdams ngag dang bcas pa Rje btsun Grags pas mdzad pa
13. Dpal mgon 'Phags pa Klu sgrub (f. 34v) kyis mdzad pa'i
Mchod rten drung thob bam Sems thag bcad pa'i man
ngag gi gsal byed Grags pas mdzad pa
14. slob doon Ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa'i Phyag rgya
chen po yi ge med pa'i man ngag Grags rgyal gyis
mdzad pa
15. Slob dpon Tog tse pas mdzad pa'i Bsam gyis mi khyab

IV. MAR PA'I BKA' BRGYUD
(bzhi pa sgrub brgyud bstan pa'i spyi mes dgyes mdzad
sprul pa'i lo tsā ba chen po mnga' bdag mar pa'i bka'
brgyud kyi gdams ngag la gnyis/ gzhung rtsa 'grel gyi skor/
gdams ngag khrid kyi rim palo)
A. Dang po la gnyis/ (f. 35r) thun mong phyag chen gyi skor/
thun mix chos drug gi skor ro/
1. Thun mong Phyag chen gyi skor
a. Dpal mnyogs pa med pa'i rgyud
b. Bram ze chen pos mdzad pa'i dmangs do ha
c. De'i bsdus don Sbar phu bas mdzad pa
('di la lung med)
d. Sha ba ri pa'i Snying po don gyi man ngag
e. Te lo pa'i Phyag chen ganggā ma
f. De'i sa bcad dang 'grel pa Kun mkhyen Rang byung
rdo rjes mdzad pada
Nā ro pa'i Phyag chen tshig bsdus
De'i 'grel chung rtogs par slaba Rje bla ma 'Jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos mdzad pa
i. Mai tri pa'i De kho na nyid bcu pa
j. Mar pa'i Yid la mi byed pa'i mgur rtsa
k. Rie btsun Mi la'i Ye shes gsal byed
1. Sgam po pa'i Lam gcig chod bcas
aty Phyag chen rgya gzhung grub pa sde bdun gtsor gyur
pu sti gnyis tsam lung rgyun bcas bzhugs par snang
yang 'dir brgyud pa 'di dang 'brel mtshungs mtshon
byed tsam bkod pa'o/
Thun min Chos drug gi skor
a. Bka' yang dag pa'i tshad ma Ye shes mkha' 'gro'i
gsung
b. Snyan brgyud rdo rje'i tshig rkang Rgyal ba Rdo
rje 'chang gi bka'
('ai la brtag byar smra ba ni phyogs zhen tsam du
zad
?c. De'i 'grel chung Rdo rje'i tshig 'byed
d. Chos drug gi ka dpe che chung gnyis
e. Tai lo pa'i Chos drug man ngag
f. Nā ro pa'i Chos drug rdo rje'i mgur
g. Rje btsun Mi la'i snyan brgyud gsal ba skor gsum
bcas
B. Gdams ngag khrid kyi rim pa
(gnyis pa gdams khrid kyi rim pa la gnyis) smin byed dbang/
grol byed khrid gzhung dngos so)
1. Smin byed dbang
a. Bka srol 'dir rtsa ba'i smin byed bde mchog yab yum
gang rung la brten cing de'ang Nā ro lugs gtso bor
mdzad pa mthun kyang lugs srol de la snyan brgyud
thun mong ma yin pa dang/ thun mong bka' brgyud so
so'i bka' srol las byon pa'i rnam grangs mang du
bzhugs pa las 'dir spyi tsam du bka' brgyud rtsa ba
Dwags po lugs kyi bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang gi
sgrub akyil Bkra shis mam rgyal gyis mdzad pa tsam
bzhugs/
Grol byed khrid gzhung
(gnyis pa la gnyis/ rtsa ba snyan brgyud kyi chos skor
las byung ba dang/ bka' (f. 35v) brgyud so so las byon
pa'i yig cha rnams so)

B.
• V. SHANGS PA BKA' BRGYUD
(inga pa sa bcu'i dbang phyug ye shes dā ki rnam gnyis
kyi zhal lung gtso bor gyur pa'i dpal ldan shangs pa bka
brgyud kyi gdams skor la gsum/ rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig
rkang 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i skor/ smin byed dbang dang
byin rlabs/ grol byed khrid kyi skor ro/)
A. Dang po ni/rtsa ba chos drug/ 'sdong po phyag chen/'yal ga
lam khyer/''bras bu'chi med dang bcas pa'i rdo rje tshig
rkang 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i skor/*me tog mkha' spyod
rtsa ba/
Gnyis pa ni/'byin rlabs sgo 'byed kyi bka' gnyis/'byin
rlabs khog dbub kyi (f. 37r) bka' gnyis/byin rlabs
gzhung shing gi bka' drug/ gzhung bka' phyi ma rnams
kyi byin rlabs kyi yi ge zhwa lu mchog sprul gyis mdzad
pa/
'Bde mchog lha Inga'i mngon rtogs/ 'akyil chog/ 'tshogs kyi
cho ga/ sgrub thabs kyi mnam bshad mams rje btsun rin
po che tā ra nā thas mdzad pa/
Rgyud sde lnga gtso bsdus kyi' sgrub thabs rje btsun rin
po ches mdzad pa/
Dkyil chog nyung bsdus/
Bsnyen yig zab don snying po/
c. Gsum pa ni/
Grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal pos md zad pa'i
chos drug khrid kyi gnad yig snying po kun 'dus/
Phyag chen gwa'u ma/
Lam khyer gsum/
Lam sems 'chi med/
Bla mgon dbyer med kyi khrid/
"Ring brgyud dang nye brgyud gnyis kyi gsol 'debs gnas
sbyar ma/
vchos drug khrid yig zab don thang mar brdal ba/
Gzhung khrid ma mo 'i lhan thabs kha skong/
✓ Khrul 'khor rtsa tshig rnams rje btsun sgrol mgon zhabs
kyis mdzad pa/
chos drug stan thog gcig ma'i khrid yig ye shes dā ki'i
zhal lung/
Phyag chen gwa'u ma'i khrid yig rje btsun rin po ches
mdzad pa/
Mkha' spyod akar dmar gyi nyams len dbu ma'i mdud 'grol/
Mkha' spyod dkar mo'i bstod pa di pam ka ras mdzad pa/
Mkha' spyod dkar dmar gyi 'pho khrid yig mying/
Su kha siddhi'i chos skor rgya gzhung/
Su kha chos drug gi brgyud 'debs de chen char 'bebs/
Chos drug gi khrid yig zung 'jug myur lam)
Lha bzhi dril sgrub kyi khrid yig ye shes 'od 'phro
Nyams len ye shes rang gsal/
Gser chos inga'i sngon rjes ngag 'don rdo rje'i tshig
rkang byin rlabs 'od 'bar/
Rtsa tshig 'khrul med rdo rje'i rgya mdud/
Shangs pa bka' brgyud kyi bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga yid
bzhin nor bu
Brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rdo rje 'bebs pa/
Shangs lugs mkha' 'gro sde Inga'i rjes gnang/
Myur mdzad ye shes mgon po'i byin rlabs bka" chen bcu
gsum gyi yig cha gsar spel/
Mgon po snying zhugs kyi byin rlabs (f. 37v) dang khrid
kyi yi ge/
kşe tra pā la'i rjes gnang phyag drug pa'i gtor chog dang
kha skong bcas/

VI. ZHI BYED
(drug pa grub pa'i dbang phyug dam pa sangs rgyas la bka'
bka' babs pa'i dam chos sdug bsngal zhi byed kyi skor la
gnyis/ dngos dang/ yan lag go)
A. DNGOS
(dang po la gsum/ rtsa ba/ dbang/ gdams khrid do)
1. RISĀ BA
Gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyud sde'i dum bu
mchan 'grel dang bcas pa/
Lam dri ma med pa dngui sgong dag pa'i skor/
Gser sgong dag pa'i skor/
Shel sgong dag pa'i skor/
Zhal gdams ding ri brgyad cu/
Rje btsun mi la ras par gnang ba'i rdo rje'i mgur sa
bcad dang bcas pa/
DBANG
Bka' babs dang po kha che lugs kyi sgron ma rnam gsum
dbang/
Lha gsum gyi rjes gnang/
Bka' babs bar pa rma lugs phyag chen dbang/
So lugs bla ma'i byin rlabs/
Kam lugs sher phyin ma'i rjes gnang/
Bka' babs phyi ma dam pa kun dga'i lugs kyi lam Inga'i'
glegs bam gyi dbang rgyas pa/
Řten 'brel bdag gtod dam pa'i byin rlabs/.
Thugs dam bde gshegs bcu gnyis kyi dbang/
Mgon po a gho ra'i rjes gnang/
zhing skyes kun tu ri ka dang nor bu bzang po'i rjes
gnang dang bcas kyi yi ge lo chen dharma shrīs mdzad pa/
3. Gsol 'debs gser phreng ma/
Zhi byed snga phyi bar gsum gyi khrid yig phyogs bsdebs
bdul rtsibi nying khu lo chen gsung/
Zhi byed lam inga'i khrid yig snye mdo bsod nams dpal
gyis mdzad pa/
Dam pa'i smon lam sum cu/
Kun dga'i smon lam bcu gsum/
Zhi byed bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga bcas/
B. YAN LAG
(gnyis pa yan lag dam chos bdud kyi GCOD YUL gyi skor
la gsum/ gzhung rtsa ba/ sgo 'byed dbang/ gdams ngag khrid
kyi rim pa'o)
1. GZUNG RTSA BA
Bram ze ār.ya de ba'i gzhung tshigs bcad chen mo/
De'i gzhung 'grel zag med sbrang rtsi drung pa ru pas
mdzad pa/
Ma gcig gi bka' tsḥoms chen mo/
De'i sa bcad dang 'grel pa rang byung zhabs kyis mdzad
Yang tshoms zhus (f. 38r) lan ma/
Nying tshoms chos kyi rtsa ba/
Thun mong gi le lag brgyad/
Thun mong min pa'i le lag brgyad/
Khyad par gyi le lag brgyad/
Shes rab skra rtse'i sa gzhung spel ba/
Zab don thugs kyi snying po'i gzhung/
2. SGO 'BYED DBANG
Zur mang lugs kyi gtor dbang/

kho na ma yin pa]

MỘT
Sgrub brgyud shing rta chen po brgvad kyi smin grol snying po
phyogs gcig bsdus pa gdams ngag rin po che'i mdzod kyi dkar chag
bkra shis grags pa i rgya mtsho
fylograph
Author: Kong-sprul cu
Edition: Dpal-spungs
(Vol. A of the Gdams ngag mdzod in 10 volumes)
/rtsa ba dang brgyud par bcas pa'i dpal idan bla ma dam pa rams
la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su mchilo/
/mkhyen bzang thugs chud srid dang zhi ba'i pha mtha' rab brgal
ye shes sku/
amigs med brtse bas longs spyod sprin bkod sprul pa'i char 'bebs
gzhom med gsung/
7rtog bral nus pas 'khor ba'i g.yul zlog gnyis 'dzin 'tshing good
zab gsal thugs,
/gsang ba bsam yas rigs brgya'i khyab bdag rdo rje sems angos
bla mar 'dud/
/rab 'byams akyil 'khor ma lus 'phro ba'i gzhi/
Zsngags dang rgyud kyi 'byung gnas e wam dngos/
Abde chen gar gyis gsang mchog dgyes pa na/
rol mdzad brgyud par bcas pas byin riabs stsol/
/nyin mor byed las snang ba'i dpal bzhin tu/
srid zhi'i gnas na phun tshogs ci yod pa
Zde kun rin chen gsum las rtag byung bas/
Zreyu mtshan shes pa'i dad pas skyabs su bsnyen/
Zmkhas dang grub pa'i phrin las bsam yas pas/
lung dang rtogs pa'i bstan pa phags bod du/
Zyongs su brdal ndzad mdo sngags shin rta che il
rnam thar rgya mtshor bsngags brjod me tog 'bul/
/zhi dang chags dang (f. lv)'bar ba chen po sogs/
dngos gcig du ma'i nyams kyis gdul dka' mnams/
Z'dul mdzad thugs rje'i gar mkhan yi dam lhas/
l'dod don mtha' ru phyin pa'i dngos grub stsol)
Mye shes mkhar reyu legs nyes stangs 'dzin pa/
gnas gsum mkha' 'gro dam can chos skyong rnams/
/tha tshig gnyan dgongs gang ba i skabs phye zhing
7gegs byed tshar chod skal ldan rjes 'dzin mdzod/
kha ba can ljongs yongs su grags pa yi/
sgrub brgyud shing rta che brgyad rjes 'brangs bcas/
Zgdams ngag zab dgu'i nor bu kun tshang ba'i/
sngon med ngo mtshar md zod kyi sgo chen dbye/
7'dir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dam pa'i chos thams cad kyi nying
khu/ mdo dang rgyud kyi zab don nyams len gyi rim pa mtha' dag
tshang ba med pa/ dbang po rab 'bring tha ma gsum ka'i blo dang
'tshams shing jug bde ba/ myur ba nyid du byang chub chen po'i
go 'phang mngon du byed pa'i sgrub thabs zab mo mtha' dag phyogs
gcig tu bsdus pa gdams ngag rin po che'i mdzod chen po'i dkar
chag mdor bsdus bkod pa la don lnga/
1. mdzod chen bsdu ba'i dgos ched/
2. bka' (f. 2r) srol 'phags bod du ji ltar byung ba/
3. bstan pa'i ngo bo ngos bzung ba/
4. chos kyi rnam grangs ji tsam bzhugs pa/
5. de nyid gang las brgyud pa'i rim pa smos pa'o/
/dang po la bzhi/ gang zhig begrub par bya ba/ gang gis
sgrub pa'i thabs/ gang la ji ltar 'jug pa/ de ltar bsgrubs pa'i
dgos pa dang phan yon smos pa'o)
7dang po ni/ gang gi tshe/ sgron me'i bskal pa bzang po 'dir



rgyal ba nyi ma 'jig rten du byon pa thams cad kyi nang nas
thugs bskyed go cha gzhan las khyad par du 'phags shing/ rtsod
dus kyi gdul bya ma bsgral ba mnams sgrol ba'i mdzad pa kun
las kyang rmad du byung ba bdag cag gi ston pa thugs rje chen
po dang ldan pa mnyam med shākya'i dbang po zhes mtshan tsam
thos pas kyang bskal chen brgyad khri'i sdig pa las rnam par
grol zhing byang chub kyi lam las phyir ni idog par 'gyur ba'i
smon lam mnga' ba gang gi bstan pa rin po che 'jig rten na 'tsho
zhing gzhes pa dang/ de las kyang dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas

I. SNGA GYUR RNYING MA
(dang po bstan pa snga dar skabs su byon pa'i zab chos
thun mong ma yin pa YO GA GSUM du bzhugs pa'i...)
A. Dang po MA HA YO GA'I SKOR la
1. Sangs rgyas gsang ba'i lam chung
2. Slob doon rin poches mdzad pa'i Man ngag 1ta ba'i
phreng ba
3. De'i 'grel pa Nyi ma'i 'od zer
4. Ma mo las kyi thig le
5. Kun mkhyen Dri med 'od zer gyis mdzad pa'i Sgyu 'phrul
snying po'i don khrid rnams so/
B. Gnyis pa A NU:YO GA'I SKOR la
*1. Bde gsal mdzad kyi mal 'byor bzhi rim
2. 'Dus pa mdo las phyungs pa'i ngang sgom gyi khrid
3. Dongs sprugs kyi khrid yig zab lam snang byed Lo chen
Dharma shris mdzad pa mams so/
C. Gsum pa A TI YO GA'I SKOR la gsum sems klong man ngag go
1. Dang po phyi SEMS SDE'I SKOR la
a. Kun byed rgyal po'i rgyud las le'u so bdun pa khol
phyungs mchan bcas
b. Sems sde'i slob dpon bco brgyad kyi rdo rje'i glu
c. Snying po'i bstan boos byang chub sems sgom pa rdo
la gser zhun 'Jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa
*d. Sems sde ma bu bco brgyad kyi dgongs pa ngo sprad
pa'i thabs rig pa'i rtsal abang gi cho ga Kah thog
pa Rmog ston Rdo rje dpal bzang pos mdzad pa
e. Kun byed rgyal po'i don khrid Klong chen rab 'byams
bzang pos mdzad pa
'f. Nyang lugs khrid yig Sog zlog pa Blo gros rgyal
mtshan gyis mdzad pa
Brgyud 'debs de nyid kyi gsung la Smin gter gyis
kha skong can
'h. Khams lugs kyi khrid Kah thog pa Nam mkha' rdo rjes
mdzad pa
'i. A ro lugs kyi khrid yig Zhwa dmar Mkha' spyod dbang
pos mdzad pa rnams so/
2. Gnyis pa nang KLONG SDE'Í SKOR la
a. Klong chen rab 'byams chen po'i rgyud kyi snying po
le'u bzhi pa khol phyungs mchan can
b. Rdo rje zam pa'i gzhung man ngag zhal gdams dang
bcas pa Bai ro tsa nas bstan pa
c. Zam chung bsdus pa thun gcig ma
d. Bka' brgyud rin po che'i nyams kyi phreng ba
e. Byang chub sems kyi phan yon dpe drug gis mtshon nas
mgur du bzhengs pa
f. Zhal gdams rin po che'i (f. 32v) phreng ba
g. Sgom tshul b2a ma'i byin rlabs kyi lag len rgyas par
bkod pa
h. Sgom rten tshul shing gi yi ge
i. Sgom khrid kyi lag len 'oi ba jo sras kyi bcud rgya
sgom pa'i snod du blugs pa
j. Spyan snga Chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid yig
skal bzang mig 'byed rnams so
3. Gsum pa gsang ba MAN NGAG GI SDE'I SKOR la
a. 'Od gsal rdzogs pa chen po man ngag gi sde'i gnad kyi
bcud phun sangs rgyas kyi 'das rjes dang po dga' ldan/
gnyis pa gsang rol/ gsum pa bya rgod rir babs pa/

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Bka'-gdams-pa: General
/gnyis pa bka' gdams pa ni/ sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas
kyi rnam 'phrul sa gsum du grags pas khyab pa jo bo rje dpal idan
a ti sha bod du phebs/ log pa'i rgyal po glang dar mas chos rgyal
mes dbon gyi bstan pa bsnubs pa'i skyon gyis mdo 'dul nyams/
gsang sngags 'chol par spyod pa 'gogs shing thub bstan dri ma
med pa slar yang gsal bar mdzad pa'i slad du mdo sde rgyan dang
byang sa sogs kyi bstan don skyes bu gsum gyi lam rim yongs su
rdzogs pa byang chub lam gyi sgron ma mdzad/
lta ba dbu ma/ spyod pa 'dul bal gdams ngag byang chub
kyi sems rin po che gtsor ston/
rgyal ba'i bka' thams cad gang zag gcig 'tshang rgya ba'i
gdams ngag tu shar ba'i khrid srol btsugs pa las/ slob ma'i thu
bo rigs gsum sems dpa'i mam 'phrul khu mgog 'brom gsum las
spyan ras gzigs dngos 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi
slob ma sku mched gsum du grags pa'i/ pu to ba rin chen gsal
las glang shar nyi zla zung 'brel sogs gzhung drug gi bshad
srol 'dzin pa bka' gdams gzhung pa dang/ spyan snga tshul khrims
'bar las bden bzhi gdams ngag tu ston pa bya yul ba sogs brgyud
pa'i gdams ngag pa/ phu chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan las man
ngag this le bou drug gi smin grol rgyab brten gsang chos glegs
bam rin po che bcas stabs ka ba bogs las brgyud pa man ngag pa
ste gsum dang/ gzhan yang nag tsho'i bka' brgyud rgya cher
byon pas khams dbus kun tu khyab/
phyis su rang rkang 'dzin pa'i sde cung zad 'grib (f. 14v)
pa na 'jam dbyangs rnam 'phrul tsong kha pa blo bzang grags
pa'i dpal gyis bstan pa slar yang gsal bar mdzad pa'i phrin las
kyi snang bas bstan pa sa steng kun tu khyab par gyur to/

Gdans ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Lam-'bras-pa: General sobre
laya
za
B
onds
BV
/gsum pa lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa ni/ rnal 'byor dbang
phyug dpal idan chos skyong la rdo rje bdag med mas sprul pa'i
dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur) sa drug pa'i rtogs pa mngon du gyur
nas grub chen bi rü pa'am birwa pa zhes grags pa de nyid kyis
kye rdo rje'i rgyud la brten nas shar phyogs nag po pa'i don
du lam 'bras rdo rie'i tshig rkang stsal/ rgyud kyi bshad pa
bsdus pa dang/ lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag rgyas pa
gnang/ dombhi pa la rgyud bshad rgyas pa dang gdams ngag bsdus
pa gnang/
de dag las grub pa'i slob dpon rnams rim par brgyud de
byon pa las/ bod yul bstan pa phyi dar gyi lo tsā'i nang nas
mar 'gos 'brog gsum zhes gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i 'byung
khungs su byed pa'i ya gyal 'brog mi lo tsa ba shākya ye shes
kyis ga ya dha ra dang dpa' bordo rje las gzhung dang gdams
ngag yongs su rdzogs pa zhus/ grubchen mtsho skyes kyi gdams
pa sogs lam skor phyi mo brgyad po rnams kyang asan nas bod du
gnang ba'i slob ma grub thob bdun/ gzhung rdzogs pa'i slob ma
bdun/ man ngag rdzogs pa'i slob ma bzhi rnams su byon pa las
lam bras la sras slob brgyud pa gsum du byung ba'i nang tshan
se mkhar chung ba nas thob pa rab 'bring tha gsum las 'bring
po zha ma nas 'phel ba la'ang lugs srol bdun tsam byung ba
dang/ rab tu thob pa zhang ston chos 'bar las sa chen kun dga'
snying pos gsan cing snga bu phag gru dang lce sgom gyi lugs/
phyi bu la ring brgyud nye brgyud gnyis rnams byung/ gyi jo
lo tsă bas kyang ga ya dha ra las esan nas rim par brgyud pa
bcas lam 'bras lugs srol bco brgyad du grags pa byung ba las
SA LUGS nyid deng sang gi bar du phrin las dar rgyas su bzhugs
shing/ 'di (f. 15r) la'ang grub chen buddha shri las ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos gsan cing de nas rim gyis
brgyud pa NGOR LUGS tshogs bshad dang/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi
dpal ba las brgyud cing rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' mam rgyal
ba'i bka' srol lam 'bras RDZONG lugs dang/ rdo ring kun spangs
chen po las tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtshos gsan cing thugs
sras nyi zla Ita bu gnyis las brgyud pa TSHAR LUGS SLOB BŠHAD
bcas byung ba mnams kyang da lta'i bar bzhugs bzhin pa nyid
do/
spyir bla chen 'brog mi lo tsā la bka' babs pa'i lam
skor dgur grags pa'i gdans ngag khyad par can gyi thog ma/
rnal 'byor dbang phyug birwa pas ndzad pa'i lam 'bras bu dang
bcas pa'i skor ni gong du song/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad la bde
kye gsang gsum gyi rdzogs rim du 'gro ba drug/ rgyu sde spyi
'grel gnyis las thog mar kyai rdor 'grel pa lugs kyi rdzogs rim/
dombhi he na kas rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa la brten nas lhan cig
skyes grub mdzad/
gyis pa slob doon padma badzras rdo rje gur gyi rgyud
la brten nas sgrub thabs mtsho skyes mdzad pa la kyai rdor
mtsho skyes lugs su grags pa'i rdzogs rim zab pa'i tshul dgu
dang mar me'i rtse mo ita bu'i gdams ngag/
gsum pa nag po spyod pa'i rdo rjes bde mchog bshad rgyud
la brten nas nag po'i gzhung drug mdzad/ de dag gi nang nas o

/gsum pa lam 'bras ni/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i rgyad gsum gyi

/bzhi pa MNGA' BDAG MAR PA'I BKA' BRGYUD ni/ dpal te lo
pa chen pos ring brgyud 'phags pa klu sgrub dombhi pa lu yi

80 so las gsan pas bka' babs bzhi'i mnga' bdag tu gyur/ sgrub

bka' babs/ mi la'i slob ma mkha' spyod du gshegs pa bdun/ ras

GZHUNG RTSA 'GREL GYI SKOR: THUN MONG PHYAG CHEN GYI SKOR
Includes:
a) Rgyud kyi Fgyal po mnyog pa med pa zhes bya ba.

Incipit: /rgya gar skad du/ a nā ni la tantra rā dza na ma/

zhing bdag med dag pa nyid] /mtshan med mtshan gzhi mnam

bsdus pas/ /bdag gis gsal bar bshad pa yin/ /rmongs pa mnams
la phan 'dod pas/ /snying rjes 'di ni bstan pa yin/...
Terminatur: /dpal bde ba dam pa rtogs par byed pa dang ldan
pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud byin gyis brlabs pa'i rim pa chen po
mkha' 'gro ma drwa ba sdom pa'i brtags pa mnyogs pa med pa

ya dha ra dang/ /bod kyi 10 tsā ba dge slong shākya ye shes
kyis bsgyur ba''o/(/'di ni spros padang bcas pa'i spyod pa

bsgyur ba'ang yod/ (mchan))
b) Do ha mdzod kyi glu.
ff. 4r-llv (pp. 7-22)
Incipit: /rgya gar skad du/ /do ha ko sa grā ti/ /bod skad
du/ /do ha mdzod kyi glu/ /'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la
phyag 'tshal lo/ /dug sbruí ita bu'i skal med ni] Anges par
skye bo dam pa la/ /skyon gyi dri mas dgod pa'i phyir/ /mthong
ba tsam gyis 'jigs par byos/
Terminatur: /de bas bdag nyid bor bar byas na rung/ /rnal
'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dpal sa ra ha chen po'i zhal
snga nas mdzad pa do ha mdzod ces bya ba de kho nyid rnal
du mtshon pa don dam pa'i yi ge rdzogs so/ (/phyag rgya chen
po snying po'i don gyi gdams pa'i shing rta chen po 'phags
yul gyi grub pa'i dbang phyug mtha' dag gi gtsug gi nor bu
bram ze chen po dpal sa ra ha zhes pa 'jig rten na nyi zla

cing sbyor ba'i yum/ /bde ster dpa' mo khyod la phyag 'tshal
nas/ /snyan brgyud lhan cig skyes ma'i mngon dkyil gyi/ chog
grigs gong ma'i man ngag bzhin du bri/ de yang bcom ldan

dkyil 'khor du dbang dang sdom pa thob cing dam tshig dang
idan pa'i maal 'byor pas) spros med zab mo sindhu ra rdo rje

du abang bskur ba'i rim pa la gsum/ sbyor ba dang/ 'jug pa
dang/ rjes so

legs so/

Phyaga chen
Incipit: /bla ma dam pa mnams la phyag 'tshal lo/. /yang dag

pa dang/ rtog ge'i gzhung gi tshig ma bsres par bris pa'o/

Itar du bstan/ kha cig rtog dpyod bzhin du bshad] /de kun mi

cig skyes sbyor don /gcig shes kun grol mkhyen pa yis/ /sgra
don rtogs pas phye ba yin/ /age bas sems can thams cad kyis/

tu nyams len bya o/
/shing pho byi ba'í lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes gcig la bde chen
du sbyar ba'o/

ff. 18
Incipit: /om swa sti si ddhi hūm/ nyams rtogs yon tan thams

cig skyes sbyor zhes grags pa 'di nyid nyams su len par byed
pa la/ sngon 'gro/ dngos gzhi/ rjes dang gsum
Colophon: /zhes pa 'di lugs gnyis kyis mngon par mtho ba/ d pal
ldan bla ma'i thugs sras su gyur pa'i gu'i gung pa nang so
mchod sprin pas dgos zhes bskul bar brten zin thun du sku rab
bkra shis sgang nas badzre shwa ras bris shing spel ba'o/ /bkra
shis dpal 'bar nyams rtogs 'bar zhing bstan pa rgyas pa'i
rgyan du byon/ thun sum cu so gcig yod/...
Author: Karma-pa IX Dbang-phyug-rdo-rje (1556-1603).
5. Sgrab brgyud karma kam tshang pa'i phyag chen lhan cig skyes
sbyor gyi sngon 'gro bzhi sbyor sogs kyi ngag 'don 'phags lam
bgrod pa'i shing rta
Margins: (v) Karma kam tshang
(r) Ca Sngon -- gro
ff. 9

Probably compiled by Kong-sprul Blo-gros-mtha'-yas (1813-1899).

seng Ideng stug po'i nag gseb tu begyur zhing zhus te gtan

byang 'god par mdzad do/
/bskyed rim lhan cig skyes pa'i lha khrid ji ltar nyams su

pa bzhin dpal gtsug lag phreng bas bshad pa legs par grub po/

rnam pa tha dad Itar snang yang ngo bo tha dad med par gnas
lugs nges par bya ba ni gzhi ngos bzung ba'o/

10. Chos drug bdud rtsi nying khu'i sngon 'gro dngos grub myur
stsol.

ff. 4
Incipit: /om swa sti si dahi hüm rab 'byams akyil 'khor kun
bdag 'khor io'i mgon) /rdo rje 'chang dbang dpal ldan karma
pa/ /rnam kun 'bral med rigs kyi bdag por brten/ /agongs pa
gro] zhing rjes su gnang bar gsol/ 7de la 'air rgyal ba kun

nas snyan du brgyud pa'i byin rlabs kyi tshan kha ma nyams
pa gang zag las dang skal bar ldan pa dag gis nyams su len
pa'i rim pa la/ dang po thun mong gi sngon 'gro dal 'byor

Gdang ngay mdzod (Ca)

'dud/ /gza' bral sprin gyis dag pa'i nyi zla ltar/ Longs

rgyal bsgom/ bzhi pa sems nyid sangs rgyas su ngo sprod/ Inga
pa dge ba'i rtsa ba rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bsngo bao/
Terminatur: /rje btsun dwags po rin po che'i zhal gdams
rdzogs so/ /zhes khro phu lo tsā ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal
gyi gsung rab man ngag brgya rtsa las byung ba'o7

18
/dpal ldan 'jigs med bdud las rgyal ba yi/ /bshes gnyen bla

cang shes 'di zhon "bros par gyis/...
Terminatur: /ces pa 'di ni gtsang stod sa'i thig le dpal ldan
sa skya'i byad 'dabs su skyes pa) sdom brtson sde snod 'dzin
pa 'dzims dkar nyi zla rab 'byams kyis nye bar bskul ba'i
ngor/ shākya'i dge slong chos smra ba/ 'brug pa rin po che'i

43. 'Brug pa rin po che'i khrid chung brgyad kyi gdams pa kun la
med pa'i khyad chos bzhugs so.
Margins: (v) 'Brug lugs khrid chung
Tr) Ca Khyad -- chos
ff. 10
Incipit: /na mo ma hā mu drā ya/ de la yang dag par rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas mnams gaul bya rang gi bsam pa dang mthun
par gang la gang dul ba'i chos kyi sgo ji snyed cig gsungs
pa thams cad don dang bcas pa kho na ste7 theg pa sna tshogs
thabs tshul gyis/ /'gro ba'i don la rtogs pa po/ /zhes pa
dang/ bsam pa'i khyad par ji bzhin du/ 7sems can rnams la
bshad par 'tshal/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin du/ khyim pa dang/
rab tu byung ba dang/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la zhugs
pa dang/ gsang sngags kyi mal 'byor spyod pa rnams la/ gang
dang gang gi skabs su gsungs pa'i rtags dang/ cha lugs dang/
spyod lam thams cad rang rang gi lam gyi dngos gzhi mtshon
pa'i rjes dran du gyur pa yin
khyad par gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa na/ brda dang thabs
khyad par can gyi sgo nas/ bya ba mtha' dag sangs rgyas kyi
lam du angos su rdzogs par byed pa'i lam yin zhing/ ji ltar
snang ba'i spyod yul du gyur pa thams cad la 'di dag ni tha
mal gyi dngos por rang ga'am snyam du bsam par mi byed cing/
mos pa lam byed dang/ ye shes kyi mnam par rol pa sna tshogs
pa nyid du rjes su dran par byed pas na mnam pa lam byed
dang/ de thams cad rang gi ngo bo nyid bcos ma ma yin pa'i
de kho na nyid mngon du gyur pa las gzhan du mi 'da' bas
mngon sum lam byed de/ de lta bu'i sgo nas yid ches pa'i gnas
su blta bar bya'o/
1) Mig ra'i chos; 2) Gnyen po dung chos; 3) Sgom thag rab gnas;
4) Phreng ba byin rlabs; 5) Cog chos; 6) Dra chos; 7) Zhwa
chos; 8) 'Brug pa'i ja mchod.
Terminatur: ...dpal ngag gi dbang po'i sde zhes bya bas/
lho brag mkhar chu de wi ko ţi zhes bya ba'i gzhal med khang
chen po'i rtse mo dpal byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug ste
smras pa'o/
a) Cog chos rin chen shel gyi sgrom bu (ff. 4r-5v)
b) Dra chos rin c hen padma rwa ga'i bang mdzod (ff. 5v-7v)
c) Zhwa chos rin chen dbang, gi rgyal po (ff. 7v-8v)
d) 'Brug pa'i ja chos (sic!) (ff. 8v-iov)
Each have separate colophons. See dkar-chag of gsung-'bum of
'Brug-chen II Rgyal-dbang Kun-dga'-dpal-'byor (1428-1476).

long tsam yi ger bkod pa'o/
b) 'Pho ba hüm dmar ma (ff. 7v-10v)

ni/ rje mar pa lo tsā ba la dge bshes rngog chos rdor

su/ spyir du yang gdams ngag mang du gnang/ khyad par du

khyad par du gyur pa mi la la gnang ba bya ba yin/ bka
brgyud 'pho ba'i gdams ngag tsam na 'di las zab pa med pa
bya ba yin no/
Terminatur: /pho ba hūm dmar ma'i zhal gdams/ dpal yang
dgon pa'i 'ol 7dgeo/ ithi/ rgya rgya rgya/

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Shangs-pa Dkar-brgyud : General
lnga pa shangs pa bka' brgyud ni/ rgyal ba nyan thos rdzu
'phrul chen po zhes lung bstan pa'i mkhas grub khyung po mal
'byor pa de nyid thog mar yab chos bon dang mying ma la rim
gyis zhugs te so sor mkhas shing nus pa brnyes kyang byang chub
spyod pa'i smon lam dus su son pa'i stobs kyis de tsam gyis thugs
ma tshims te 'phags yul du byon/ rdo rje gdan pa sogs rtsa ba'i
bla ma mnam bzhi gtso bor gyur pa'i mkhas grub brgya dang inga
bcu'i zhabs la gtugs te mdo sngags kyi chos mtha' yas pa gsan/
khyad par rdo rje 'chang las (f. 17r) dngos su chos gsan cing
dag pa i sa gsum la bzhugs pa ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu ma
dang/ su kha siddhi angos su mjal zhing gdams pa zab mo bstsal
bas sku'i gnas lngar rgyud sde lnga dngos su grub pas mtshon/
mda' bsnun zhabs sogs mchog gi grub chen rnams dang dbyer mi
phyed pa'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen por gyur/
gtsang 8.yas ru shangs kyi zhang zhong du gdan sa mdzad pas
bla ma shangs pa dang/ brgyud 'dzin rnams la'ang shangs pa
bka' brgyud du grags/ dgung lo brgya dang Inga bcur bzhugs shing
gdul bya bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin grol mdzad pas bshes gnyen
khri phrag bco brgyad la sogs pa'i bu slob rnams kyi gtso bo snga
bu Inga dang phyi bu drug po mnams yin cing/ de las rdo rje
'chang gi gsang tshig chig brgyud kyi bka' babs ni rmog 1cogs
pa rin chen brtson 'grus kho na yin la/ de nas rim bzhin dbon
ston skyer sgang pa/ sangs rgyas gnyan ston/ 'gro mgon ston pa'i
bar du brgyud/ chig brgyud rdo rje'i rgya rdo rje 'chang dang
ye shes dā kis lung bstan pa bzhin du rin chen bdun pa chos
rje ston pas bkrol te grub thob kyi slob mas dzambu'i gling dang
gling phran pa tshun chad khyab par mdzad pa las/ brgyud 'dzin
gtso bo gtsang ma shangs ston/ bsam sdings pa gzhon nu grub/
jag chen rgyal mtshan 'bum ste mkhas grub rnam pa gsum gyis gdams
ngag yi ger bkod/
jag bsam gnyis kyi gdan sa slob brgyud mtha' yas pa byung/
gtsang ma shangs ston slob ma khyung po tshul mgon sogs rin chen
rnam bdun phyi mar grags pa'i skyes chen khyad par can byon,
gzhan yang chos rje ston pa'i dngos slob gser gling pa
bkra shis dpal las gyes pa dang/ la stod dkon mchog mkhar gyi
slob brgyud las gyes pa sogs mtha' yas shing/ phyis su grub
chen thang stong rgyal pos stod brgyud smad brgyud so sor gsan
nas nyams su bzhes pas ye shes mkha' 'gro dngos kyis rjes (f.
17v) su bzung ba'i nye brgyud rim pa gsum byung bas da Ita'i
bar rgyun bzhugs pa dang/ rje btsun grol mchog zhabs kyis ring
brgyud rnam grangs nyer bzhi gsan/ nye brgyud dā kis gdams pa
dngos su stsal ba'i ngo mtshar shin tu nye brgyud bcas pa
brgyud pa'i rnam grangs nyer lnga rje btsun tā ra nā tha'i
khrid yig 'dir 'du ba yin la/ mkhas grub khyung po'i khyad par
gyi chos skyong myur mdzad ye shes mgon po'i chos skor ni sngon
dus stod lugs pas phal cher là khyab/ phyis dus ri gong nas
brgyud pa'i smad lugs pas grub mtha' phal mo cher khyab cing
khyad par rje rin po che yab sras rnams kyis chos skyong gi gtso
bor mdzad pas dbus gtsang khams gsum rgya sog yan chad du mchod
bstod sgrub phrin gyis khyab/ gser chos rtsa ba rnams ni rkang
tshugs pa'i lugs 'azin deng sang shin tu dkon par snang ngo/

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Shangs-pa Bka'-brgyud: Essentials
Inga pa shangs pa bka' brgyud ni/ spyir mthar thug Inga
idan mkhas grub khyung pos 'phags yul gyi mkhas grub brgya dang
lnga bcu'i thugs bcud rdzogs par bzhes pas chos kyi sgo mtha'
yas shing 'gran zla dang bral bar grags pas phyogs gcig tu tshad
bzung gi nges pa bral yang/ rigs bsdu na bshad rtsod sgrub pa'i
lam rim ste bka' srol gsum du byon pa'i phyi ma la'ang/ ni gu ma
'i chos skor/ su kha siddhi'i chos skor/ rdo rje gdan pa'i chos
skor/ mai tri pa'i chos skor/ rā hu la'i chos skor te rnam
grangs lngar bzhugs pa'i gtso bo ye shes dā ki ni gupta'i chos
skor la'ang shangs pa bka' brgyud pa mnams kyis rgyas pa rgya
gar mkha' 'gro'i khyad 'phags kyi gdams pa bco Inga/ bsdus pa
lus gsum gyi gdams pa/ shin tu bsdus pa sems 'chi med rang grol
kho nar bsdu ba sogs yod kyang/ gcig brgyud rdo rje'i rgya ldan
eyi bka' srol yongs grags su shangs pa'i gser chos rnam inga
zhes/
rtsa ba ni gu chos drug) sdong po phyag rgya chen po/ yal
ga lam khyer mam gsum/ me tog mkha'' spyod dkar dmar/ 'bras bu
chi med chug med bcas rdo rje 'chang dang ye shes mkha' 'gro'i
rdo rje'i tshig rkang la gdams ngag dmigs pa'i thems yig tu
btab pas dmigs rkang dang gsol 'debs tsam yang gang zag gi blos
bcos bsgyur bsre bslad byar med pa gser zhun ma lta bu'i thog
ma chos drug ni/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang las/
dbang bzhis smin byas dad dang brtson 'grus ldan/
mi rtog skyo shas nyes dmigs sngon 'gro bas/
1am mchog 'di la (f. 26v) gang gis 'bad gyur na/
zla drug lo'am tshe 'dir 'tshang rgya 'gyur/ /ces gsungs
pa ltar rgyud chen rin chen rgya mtsho las gsungs pa'i rgyud
sde lnga'am dpal 'khor lo sdom pa i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
cing so so'i byin rlabs kyi bka' nos pas smin cing thun mong gi
sngon 'gro legs par 'byangs pa'i gang zag gis nyams su blang
bya'i dang po/ dag byed a'i stong ras rgyud sbyang/ de nas thabs
lam bde drod rang 'bar/ sgyu lus chags sdang rang grol/ rmi lam
nyid 'khrul rang dag/ od gsal gti mug rang sangs bzhi po rtsa
bar byas nas gnas skabs bzhi'i 'khrul pa'i dri ma bsal/ 'pho
ba ma bsgoms 'tshang rgya/ bar do rgyal ba longs sku gnyis brtson
'grus dang dbang po dman pa'i sgom rim gyi cha lag tu btang bas
mchog 'bring dman pa'i rim pas bar do gsum la mam par grol bar
gyur ro/
/phyag chen ni/ yid la mi byed pa snying po don gyi gdams
pa'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang mams mkhas grub khyung pos shin tu
thugs brtsigs che bas shog dril bal po'i gwa'u snying 'dra ba
zhig gi nang du bcug nas mgul bar 'chang bas phyag chen gwa'u
mar grags pa ni/ sngon 'gro rang babs gsum gyis zhi gnas dang
lhag mthong bskyed/ dngos gzhi rdo rje'i ye shes 'bebs pas rku
thabs su ngo sprad cing skyon bzhi rang sar grol ba'i sgo nas
sems nyid kyi gdar sha bcad/ rjes sku gsum rang shar gyi ngang
bskyang zhing thun mong ma yin pa'i bogs 'don dang gegs sei brten
pas mdo rgyud thams cad kyi bstan bya'i snying po/ man ngag thams
cad kyi nying khu/ phyag rgya chen po sku bzhi rang grol mngon
tu 'gyur ba dang/ snang grags rtog pa'i chos thans cad bla ma yi
dam sgyu ma gsum gyi rang bzhin gnad dang ldan pas lam du khyer
bas lo zla tsam gyis gsal stong bde chen sku gsum rang shar du
'byung ba dang/ bcom idan 'das ma rdo rje btsun mo nyi zla'i mdaris
'dzin khyad 'phags gsol 'debs (f. 27r) dang dmigs pa'i gnad kyis
bskul zhing 'khor lo'i gnas bzhir chags grol so so la brten pa'i
bde stong gi tsanda li sbar bas rten de nyid kyis zung 'jug chen
po'i mkha' la spyod par 'gyur ba dang/ 'chi med grub pa'i 'khrul
khor sum bcu rtsa gnyis kyis lus thar pa'i lam du gzud/ rang



sems gdod ma nas ma skyes pas "chi med rang grol chen por grub/

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Zhi-byed-pa: General
/drug pa zhi byed yan lag dang bcas pa ni, rgya gar be twa'i
yul gyi tsa ta seng ngar sku 'khrungs pa'i mkhas pa chen po ka
ma la shī la'am bod dang rgya nag tu pha dam pa sangs rgyas su
grags pa des grub thob pho mo lnga bcu nga bzhi las gdams pa zab
mo mtha' dag gsan nas rtse gcig tu sgrub pa mdzad pas bcud len
sogs thun mong grub pa chen po brgyad thob pas dgung lo lnga
brgya dang bdun cu bzhugs/ thugs dam bde gshegs bcu gnyis dang/
ngo mtshar mkha' spyod kyi bla ma sum bcu rtsa drug sogs kyis
zhal gzigs/ mchog gi dngos grub mthong lam chen po'i ye shes
brnyes pa de nyid kyis rten gzhi'i gtso bo sher phyin rgyas 'bring
bsdus gsum/ āli kā li chu klung chen po'i rgyud sogs kyi don
nyams len tu dril ba7 rten sdom pa gsum ldan/ lam aka' thub kyi
srang/ 'bras bu gzhan don spyod pa ste nyid kyi rnam par thar
pa dang mthun par las can gnam gyi skar ma tsam sangs rgyas kyi
sa la bsgral bar mdzad pa'i dam chos spyi ming (?yid) sger du
chags pa sdug bsngal zhi byed ces bya ba 'di nyid la dbang (f.
18r) po'i rim pas khrid tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa mchis kyang/
dam pa nyid bod yul 'dir lan lnga tsam phebs/
zhi byed kyi brgyud pa rim pa gsum du grags che ba'i brgyud
pa dang po kha che dznyā na gu hya la zhi byed sgron ma skor
gsum gnang ba ang po lo tsā sogs nas byung ba dang/ brgyud pa
bar pa'i gtso bo rma so kam gsum ni/ rma chos kyi shes rab la
phyag chen tshig brgyud don brgyud/ so chung dge 'dun 'bar la
rig pa gcer mthong gi man ngag tshig brgyud dang don brgyud/
kam ye shes rgyal mtshan la sher phyin gyi gdams pa yas brgyud
dang mas brgyud rnams dang/ brgyud phran gsum ni/ dge bshes
grwa pa la zhi byed sgron ma dgu skor/ lce tsandra kirti la
mdo rgyud zhal sbyor gyi gdams pa/ ljang bka' gdams pa la sher
phyin yi ge med pa'i gdams ngag gnang ba dang/
brgyud pa thor bu lab sgron gcod yul gyi gdams pa sogs
gdams phran bco lnga tsam byung bar bshad/
brgyud pa tha ma ni/ dam pa rgya nag nas yar phebs ding
rir bzhugs pa'i skabs 'phrul zhig nyi shu rtsa drug/ khyad 'phags
bu chen brgya rtsa/ mdzo mo nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ gdan non gyi
slob ma bcu gnyis sogs byung ba'i so so la gnang ba'i gdams ngag
smin grol gyi rgyun srol tshad bzung du ma mchis kyang gtso bo
sgo ba'i rnal 'byor pa bzhi yin te/ shar na dam pa phyar chen
gyis bka' mdo sbyor gyi skor/ lhor badzra kro dhas rin chen don
sdeb kyi skor/ nub na dam pa phyar chung gis dum dum khrigs kyi
skor/ byang na byang chub sems dpa' kun dga's bka' cho lu'i
skor gyi bka' bsdu mdzad cing yi ger bkod]
de la brgyud pa bar pa ni bka' tha ma nges don mdo sde
rnams dang mthun la/ phyi ma ni sngags dang gtso bor mthun par
bshad/ de dag thams cad las kyang lam yongs su rdzogs pas khyad
par''phags pa ni nyid dang dgongs pa mnyam par zhal gyis bzhes
pa dam pa kun dga'i bka' srol nyid yin cing/ chos skor 'di la
thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i sde tshan rgya cher bzhugs
(f. 18v) shing/ brgyud pa gsum ka sngar dar rgyas su bzhugs par
"dug kyang deng sang mtshan tsam du gyur cing/ smin gling 10 chen
dharma shrīs 'bad rtsol chen pos rgyun gang bzhugs gsan cing yig
cha bklags chog tu mdzad pa'i bka' drin las/ brgyud pa snga
phyi bar gsum dang khyad par dam pa kun dga'i lugs kyi smin
grol rtsa ba tsam bzhugs par snang ngo/
/yan lag gcod yul la pho gcod mo good gnyis su grags pa
las/ snga ma ni/ pha dam pa sangs rgyas kyis skyo shākya ye
shes dang yar klung sma ra ser po la mdo lugs rang rkang gi
good ārya de ba'i gzhung chung lnga bcu pa'i don gdams ngag
brul tsho drug pa zhes bya ba gnang/ skyos rang gi dbon bsod nams
bla ma/ des ma gcig lab sgron la brul tsho bzhi gnang bar grags/



sma ra ser po las brgyud pa'i skor rog shes rab 'od dang mkhas
grub gzhon nu grub rnams las 'phel ba ni pho good du grags pa'o/
mo gcod ni/ yum chen mo shes rab phar phyin mi mo'i mnam
par snang ba ma gcig lab sgron nyid/ sher phyin bklags pas
stong nyid kyi Ita ba skyes/ dam pas snying gtam tshig gcig
gsungs pas rgyud grol te rang bzhin gyi rnal 'byor mar gyur/
sher phyin gyi dgongs don ma gcig nyid kyi dgongs nyams las
'khrungs pa'i gcod yul gyi lam srol rgya chen po phyes te on
gdams skor bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad pa thams cad] pha rgyud
thabs/ ma rgyud shes rab/ gnyis med don/mkha' 'gro nyams kyi
brgyud pa bzhis bsdus shing/ zhal slob grub thob pho mo brgya
dang rtsa brgyad sogs slob tshogs mang pos bod khams khyab par
gyur pa'i gtso bo bka' babs bu chen bcu drug gi phrin las kun
tu 'phel/ mdo'i brgyud 'dzin sras glang lung pa rgyal ba don
grub brgyud pa'i gtso bor gyur/ sngags kyi brgyud 'dzin thod
smyon bsam 'grub grub thob yongs grags su gyur pas gangs pa
zhes pa'i gcod brgyud khyad par can zur du byung/
zung jug brgyud 'dzin bu (f. 19r) sgom chos kyi seng ge'i
brgyud pa grub thob so so las brgyud pa mang du 'phel/
khyad par rgyal dbang rang byung rdo rjes gnam mtsho do
pa las good yul gsan cing de nas brgyud pa la ru pa'i gcod
brgyud mnams dang/ phyis su zur mang/ gnas mdo'i lugs rnams
'phel/
rje btsun skya se rtogs ldan las skyabs che dang/ tre ho
chos kyi dbang po las tre good kyi rgyun byung bas mtshon brgyud
'dzin so so las mtha' yas pa 'phel/
sras mo la lcam las rim par brgyud pa'i ring brgyud dang/
rgyal thang pa bsam gtan 'od zer gyis brgyud srol tha dad pa
mang du gsan cing ma gcig dngos dang mjal nas gdams pa stsal ba
nye brgyud rgyal thang lugs dang/ zab chos mang po slob ma rnams
la ma gnang bar gter du sbas pa phyis ma gcig nyid kyi rnam
'phrul la 'dus rdo rje sgron mas bton pa dang/ khu sgom skye
ba kun spangs brtson 'grus seng ges gter nas phyungs pa zab
cing rgya che ba bzhugs pa las/ phyi ma'i rgyun rgya ston good
rgyud da ita bar zam ma chad par snang ngo/ Darwind

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Zhi-byed: Essentials
/drug pa zhi byed ni/ de'ang zhi byed ces pa'i sgra don/ bod
du byon pa'i khrid tshul rams kyis slob ma mi dge ba'i lam las
bzlog tu bcug nas gzod sems rgyud kyi nyom mongs sbyong bar byed
pa gtso che ba las/ 'dis ni sngon las kyi dbang gis lus dman pa
dang/ nad bu can du gyur pa sogs 'phral 'phral du zhi bar byas
nas rnal 'byor la sbyor bzod par byed pas dam chos sdug bsngal
zhi byed ces spyi ming sger du chags pa ste/ yum las/
sdug bsngal thams cad rab (f. 27v) tu zhi bar byed pa'i sngags/
ces dang/ rgyud kyi rgyal po las/
sdug bsngal gsum gyi sdug bsngal zhi/ zhes sogs gsungs pa
la brten nas btags par mdzad cing/ ngo bo pha rol tu phyin pa/
sngags dang rjes su mthun pa zhes mdo rgyud thans cad kyi zab gnad
gcig tu dril ba'i gdams pa khyad par can yin la/ spyir grub pa'i
dbang phyug dam pa sangs rgyas skye med à li kā li'i sgra don la
mnga' brnyes shing/ gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pas gdul bya'i
khams dbang dang 'tshams par brda dang tshig dang don gyi chos
sgo tshad med par bstan pas lugs srol gcig tu mam par bzhag tu
med kyang/ slob ma rnams rang nyid kyi mam thar dang mthun par
rten sdom pa gsum ldan/ lam dka' thub kyi srang/ 'bras bu gzhan
don spyod pa gsum gyis 'khrid pa la phai cher mthun cing/ thog
mar zhi byed sgron ma skor gsum mázad de lhag pa'i bslab pa gsum
po dbang po dman 'bring mchog gi nyams len tu bsdus te bstan/
bod 'dir bka' babs snga phyi bar gsum du grags pa'i dang po kha
che lugs ni/ grub thob pho mo lnga bcu rtsa bzhi'i gdams pa thams
cad dpel Ingas mtshon pa'i gnad Ingar bsdus nas gsungs/
bar pa la rma so kan gsum las/ rma lugs ni don gyi brgyud
pa la brten nas lag khrid bcu drug gis ngo sprad cing/ tshig gi
brgyud pa la brten nas gnad chen bcu drug gis sgro 'dogs bead/
so lugs ni/ bzhag thabs gnad gsun dang ldan pa la rab 'bring tha
ma'i tshul gyis ngo sprad nas chings bcu dang idan pas nyams su
len/ kam lugs lakhrid srol rgya cher byung yang phyis ni sher
phyin snying po'i don khrid tsam bzhugs par snang/
bka babs phyi ma byang chub sems dpa' kun dga'i lugs/ shes
rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag/ gsang sngags dang rjes
su mthun pa/ rtsa rgyud la bskur ba snying po don gyi ngo sprod/
thabs rten 'brel gyi che ba du mas brgyan nas sangs rgyas (f. 28r)

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Sbyor-ba yan-lag drug: General
/bdun pa rdo rje'i mal 'byor sbyor ba yan lag drug pa ni/
ston pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis dpal 'bras spungs kyi
mchod rten tu rdo rje theg pa bla med kyi rtsa ba'i rgyud ntha'
dag 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i 'dus pa chen po'i
'khor rnams la bstan pa'i tshe/ sprul pa'i chos rgyal zla ba
bzang pos gsol ba btab pa'i ngor dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsa ba'i
rgyud stong phrag bcu gnyis pa gsungs pa nyid shambha la'i
yul du chos rgyal bdun rdzogs kyi bar dar rgyas su spyod/ de
nas rigs ldan 'jam dpal grags pas de las bsdus pa'i rgyud mdzad
pa la/ rig ldan padma dkar pos 'grel chen gyi bkral/ sprul pa'i
rigs ldan rim par byon pa mnams kyis spel bar mdzad pa las
'phags yul du'ang snga thog zhig nas grub chen rnams la thor
bur snang mod/ thun mong gi spyod yul du thog mar snang bar
mdzad pa po ni tsi lu pandi ta stel de nyid shambha lar sems
'grel tshol bar (f. 19v) byon pa'i lam kar rigs ldan gyi sprul
pas rjes su bzung ste dbang rgyud 'grel man ngag mtha' dag
gnang zhing byin gyis brlabs pas mtha' dag khong du chud/ de'i
slob ma pindo ā tsarya ste slob dpon bsod snyoms par grags
pa las/ dus 'khor zhabs chen po'am tsi lu pa chung bar yang
grags pa 'jam pa'i rdo rjes gsan/ sprul pa'i rigs ldan gyis
byin gyis brlabs pa'i mthus grub pa brnyes te ka lā par dngos
su phebs te dbang rgyud man ngag rdzogs par mdzau/
'di nyid rtsal du bton nas 'chad nyan mdzad pa las/ nā ro
pa/ ratnā ka ra gupta sogs slob ma mang du byung ba las/ a ba
dhū ti pa/ shri bhadra bho dhi/ nā lenda pa gsum ka la dus
zhabs chung ba so sor grags/
bod yul 'dir thog mar gyi jo lo tsā ba zla ba'i fod zer
gyis dus zhabs pa shri bha dra spyan drangs nas rgyud 'grel
bsgyur cing man ngag gsan/ khrom lo tsā ba padma od zer sogs
bu chen bzhir grags pa byung/ khrom lo las brgyud pa'i gyi jo
lugs/ nā lenda pa'i slob ma manydzu kirti/ de'i slob ma bal po
samanta shri/ de las rwa lo tsa ba chos rab kyis gsan pa'i rwa
lugs dang/ yang/ nā lenda pa'i slob ma khache zla ba mgon po/
de las 'bro lo shes rab grags/ sgom pa dkon mchog srung sogs
las brgyud pa'i 'bro lugs dang/ na lenda pa/ tswa mi sangs rgyas
grags/ de nas rim par brgyud pa tswa mi lugs/ de'i slob ma se
lo tsā ba gzhon nu tshul khrims/ de las gnyos dar ma 'od kyis
gsan pa sogs gnyos lugs/ yang/ nā lenda pa abha yā ka ra/
nişka langka/ bal po'i pandi ta re bendra/ chag lo chos rje
dpal las brgyud pa chag lo lugs/ a bha yā] bi khyā ta de ba/
kha che paſ chen shākya shri/ dpyal chos kyi bzang po nas
brgyud pa pan chen lugs sam dpyal lugs/ rwa chos rab nas/ ye
shes seng ge] 'bum seng/ rong pa rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje sogs
las brgyud pa rong lugs/ tswa mi nas khams pa rgwa lo gzhon nu
dpal/ des zhang tshal pa la gnang ba tshal lugs/ rga lo nas sa
skya pa chen po la gnang ba'i sa lugs/ (f. 20r)
grub chen sha ba ri dbang phyug gis pan chen bi bhū ti tsa
ndra la dngos su stsal/ des ko brag pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan
la gnang ba ko brag lugs/
manydzu kirti dang a bhā yas gnyan lo dang rgwa lo la
gnang/ de gnyis ka las bla ma 'gos kyis gsan pa 'gos lugs /
yang/ chag chos rje dpal ba nas/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal/
mkhas grub orgyan pa/ snye mdo kun dga' don grub/ rje rang
byung ba sogs la brgyud pa dang/ tswa mi'i lugs gtso bor bton
pa kar lugs/
gzhan yang shong dpang nas brgyud pa bo dong lugs/ lkog
'phrang ba'i lugs dang/ la stod dbang rgyal lugs sogs mang du
byon kyang/ phyis nas dus kyi 'khor lo gangs can ljongs 'dir
shin tu dar bar md zad pa ni jo zhal gnyis te/ 'di gnyis kas dang



po rwa pa'i brgyud pa las gsạn cing/ phyis su 'bro lugs la
zhugs pas rwa "bro'i brgyud 'dzin tu gyur mod/
bu lugs gtso bor bshad pa'i bka' babs pas da Ita'i bar
du'ang bu ston chen po las brgyud pa'i rgyud bshad rgyun ma
chad par bzhugs par snang ba dang/
jo nang pa rigs ldan sprul pa'i sku rim par byon pa rnams
las kun spangs chen pos bod du 'gyur ro cog gi dus 'khor lugs
srol rdzogs par gsan/ slob ma kun spangs bu bzhir grags pa byon/
kun mkhyen dol po pa chen pos rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa'i phrin
las ngo mtshar bsam gyis mi khyab pa spel ba las/ gtso bor rang
mnyam slob ma bcu bzhi po so sos gdams srol spel ba'i phrin las
rgya che la rgyun chags pas sgrub brgyud kyi bka' babs/ nyams

mtha' bar gsum/ phyis byon paſ chen nags kyi rin chen las

Gdams ngag mdzod: Dkar chag: Bsnyen sgrub: General
/brgyad pa rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub ni/ mkhas grubo
rgyan pa rin chen dpal de nyid mdo sngags kyi sbyangs pa mthar
phyin/ khyad par dus kyi 'khor lo la mkhas pa'i phul du gyur/
rgyal ba rgod tshang pa las rtogs pa mthar thug skyes te mthong
lam gyi bden pa gzigs/ chos rje kyang brtul zhugs rang dang mñam
pa'i thugs sras su bsngags pa des spyod pa mthar phyin par bya
ba'i phyir dza lendha ra sogs gnas yul mang du byon/
khyad par nub phyogs o rgyan gyi yul du byon pa na bar chad
dang cho phrul mang du byung ba lta ba'i going dang brtul zhugs
kyi zil gyis mnan) yul dbus dhū ma tha la'i phyogs bzhir rigs
bzhi mkha' 'gros byin gyis brlabs/ spral pa'i mdzes mas lung
bstan pa bzhin ka po ka zhes pa'i grong du rdo rje mal 'byor
ma nyid smad 'tshong ma'i gzugs su bstan nas bza' btung dang reg
bya'i bde ba bstsal te rtsa mdud bkrol/ sgra dang sa g.yo ba
sogs ltas chen po dang bcas slar rdo rje btsun mo angos su snang
bas gdams pa 'di rdzogs par gnang/ sngar gyi mkha' 'gro bzhi
dang seng ge'i gdong can lnga pos kyang gdams pa sna re gnang
bas mchog thun mong gi grub pa brnyes/ bod du byon nas thog mar
lung bstan thob pa i slob ma mkhar chu rin po ches gsol ba btab
pa'i ngor rdo rje'i tshig rkang yi ger bkod/ dmigs rkang gnang
ba mams brjed tho bsdus pa'ang mdzad/ khrid gnyer pa zla ba
seng ges man ngag rnams glegs bam du bsdams/ go lung pa gzhon
nu dpal gyis dri ba zhus pa'i lan 'debs gnang ba thor bkod pa
dang] zur phug pa rin chen dpal bas mdzad pa'i ţik chen dang/
mkhas pa shangs ston dang/ snye mdo kun dga' don grub gnyis
kyis rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi rnam bshad mdzad pa rnams la ţik
chen bzhi zer/
spu hrang po bsod nams 'od zer las chos rje gangs pa
brgyud dpal ldan bla ma bsod (f. 21r) nams rgyal mtshan nas
gsan pa sogs rgyun grol yang mang du byung zhing/ kun mkhyen
rang byung zhabs kyis grub chen pa nyid las gdams skor rdzogs
par gsan te rdo rje'i tshig gi mdud 'grol dang gdams ngag gi
gnad gzhan las khyad par 'phags pa'i lam bzang po gsal bar

ff. 16
Margins: (v) Khrid phran sgrol dkar
(r) A Sgrub -- rjes
Incipit: na mo gu ru bhyah 'chi med rtag pa dam pa'i snang
ba yis/ /'chi med tshe dang ye shes sbyin mdzad pa?./'chi med

ba/ dngos gzhi/ rjes so/

ma yin pa'i sgrub cing mchod pa'i cho ga'i ngag 'don snying por
dril ba 'di yang/ gnas gsar pa jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug dang/ zhwa lu mkhan chen rin po che bsod nams mchog grub/
mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub sogs lugs 'di la tshad
mar gyur pa mnams kyi gsung gi snang ba la brten nas rang gzhan
mang por phan pa'i ihag bsam mam pa dag pas kun nas bslangs te
khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i ngo bor gyur pa mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pa byams pa kun dga' bstan'azin sogs yongs 'dzin
dam pa bdun las chos tshul 'di'i bka' drin mang du thos pa'i
rgyal khams kyi bya phral ba 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
pos sbyar ba dge legs su gyur cig/

ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi cho ga gsal bar bkod pa 'chi med grub
pa'i bdud rtsi

gnang thun mong ba'i yig cha la/ snyan brgyud zhal shes kyi zin

len mdzad pa gzhi byas/ tshig gi mtha' bskyed tshul mi gal bas

po/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ mkha' 'gro mandā ra ba'am ni

pa de nyid kyis/ jigs bral dus gsum rnam mkhyen la snyan

ff. 19

(r) A Brgyud - 'debs
Incipit: om swa sti siddham/ 'di brgya'i brgyud pa'i gsol
'debs/ /brjod be brgyud pai mtshan sdom /eung Zad goal bar
bkod pa zhes bya ba/ /bla ma dang mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs
la phyag 'tshal lo
Colophon: /de ltar zab khrid brgya dang brgyad kyi bla ma
brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ brjod bde brgyud pa'i mtshan sdom zhes
pa di'ang/ nam grangs mang ba'i stobs kyi re re nas brjod na/
bri brjod 'dzin sbyang dka' tshegs che ba la bsam/ bskal
bzang rgyan phreng gi dpe ltar tshigs 'doms gang che rang gnad
kyi snying por bzung nas bris la/ bla ma rnams kyi mtshan gyi
zur rams la rtogs dogs nas mchan bus legs par bkrol zhing
gsal bar byas/ gong 'og zlos dgos pa rnams amigs su phye ste
bad pa chen pos yi ger 'bri ba'i bsam sgom tsam rgyun du yid
yul du gnas kyang/ lus kyi mnam g.yeng la le long spyod pa'i
dbang gis/ lag thog tu mi longs pa'i btang snyoms kyis gnas
pa' i skabs su bu dam tshig can rnam grol seng ge dpal bzang
pos nyin re bzhin yang/ yang yang nan gyis bskul ba'i byed pos
mtshans sbyar te/ grol mchog gi blo gros kyi rgya mtsho las
nye bar byung ba'o/...yi gę pa ni kun dga' legs rgyal gyis so/
de ltar rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog, gis mdzad pa'i brgyud
debs nyid rtsa thob snyel gsos lta bu'i tshig sna bsdus ches
pas 'dzin klog mi bde ba dang/ mchan bu mang zhig phal cher
dpe ngan rgyun 'byams su song bas gzhung nyid kyang gang yin
med pa'i skyon du gyur ba ma zad 'bri dus shin tu dka' bar
snang zhing/ mchan rkyang tsam bsdebs pa la yig tshogs ha cang
che ba mi aug pas/ brgyud pa'i mtshan ngo mi phrod pa'i rigs
mnams rtsa gzhung nyid sor bzhag/ mchan thams cad dkyus su
btsud/ dgos pa mi che ba'i mtshan tshar grangs can "dug pa
rnams dor nas brgyud pa'i kha skong bcas rtsis med kyi rnal
'byor spyod pa blo gros mtha' yas kyis bklags chog tu bsdebs
pa 'gal 'khrul nyes pa gang mchis bla ma rgyal ba sras bcas
la 'thol zhing bshags pa dang/ dge bas zab khrid brgya rtsa'i
rgyun bzang srid mtha'i bar du mi nub dar zhing rgyas pa'i
rgyur gyur cig/ /dge legs 'phel/

bstsal ba bzhin/ legs mdzad bzang po 'di nyid kyi phyogs su

28. Sgrub brgyud shing rta chen po brgyad kyi smin grol snying po
phyogs gcig bsdus pa gdams ngag rin po che'i ndzod kyi dkar
chag bkra shis grags pa'i rgya mtsho
ff. 84
Margins: (v) Brgyud yig
(r) A Dkar -- chag
Incipit: /rtsa ba dang brgyud par bcas pa'i dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa mnams la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su mchi'o/ /mkhyen
bzang thugs chud srid dang zhi ba'i pha mtha' rab brgal ye
shes sku/ /amigs med brtse bas longs spyod sprin bkod sprul
pa'i char bebs gzhom med gsung/ /rtogs bral nus pas 'khor
ba'i g.yul zlog gnyis 'dzin 'ching good zab gsal thugs/ /gsang
ba bsam yas rigs brgya'i khyab bdag rdo rje sems dngos bla mar
'dud
Colophon: /de Itar gangs can ljongs su byon pa' sgrub brgyud
shing rta chen po brgyad dang khrid tshui thor bu khyad par
'phags pa mnams las deng sang rgyun bzhugs nges pa rnams kyi
smin grol rtsa ba tsam legs par bsdus pa gdams ngag rin po
che'i mdzod kyi dkar chag dang brgyud pa mdor smos pa 'di'ang/
sangs rgyas gnyis pa guru padmā ka ra dang rdzogs pa'i sangs
rgyas dpal karma bka' brgyud kyi bstan pa'i sgor zhugs shing
thub bstan ris su ma chad pa skye ba nas skye bar 'dzin pa'i
g.yar dam 'chang ba/ dben khrod rnams su gtad med kyi mal
'byor spyod pa karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho phrin las
kun khyab dpal bzang po' am rgyal ba'i sras po blo gros mtha'
yas pa'i sdes/ mdo khams bka' brgyud kyi gdan sa chen po dpal
spungs thub bstan chos 'khor gling gi yang dben shri de biko
ti tsā 'dra rin chen brag gi sgrub gaas kun bzang bde chen
'od gsal gling du bgyis pa dge legs 'phel/
